[2;36m                    [0m         [39man attempted connection to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m while processing an XSSF file, indicating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat untrusted data from the input file can trigger external network connections, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially leading to exfiltration of sensitive data or exposure of internal [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mservices.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** vulnerability, classified as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmedium severity security issue by the Jazzer fuzzing framework. SSRF [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities occur when an application can be manipulated to make requests to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary destinations based on untrusted input data.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests during the parsing of XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExcel XML format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m files by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache POI. Specifically, the issue occurs when:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method is called to extract text [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent from an Excel file[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This triggers `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which parses XML[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperties[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The XML parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`SAXParser`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m encounters an entity reference during document [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscanning[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The entity reference causes the XML parser to attempt an external connection to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"jazze.com:80"[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. This connection attempt is intercepted by the Jazzer SSRF sanitizer, which [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mraises the security exception[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Stack Trace Analysis[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability path follows this execution flow:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Entry point: `[0m[1;35mPOIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mPOIFuzzer.checkExtractor[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Processing: `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XML parsing: `[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` chain through various Xerces internal parsers[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Entity scanning: `[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Entity resolution: `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Network connection: `[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` leading to socket [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection attempt[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Related**: The vulnerability appears to be related [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto XML External Entity processing, where entity references in XML documents can [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrigger external resource resolution[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Default XML Parser Behavior**: The Java built-in XML parsers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXerces[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing used without apparent restrictions on external entity resolution[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Vulnerable Component**: The `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` class is processing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML content with extended properties that contain potentially malicious entity [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Network Layer**: The actual network connection is attempted through standard [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava HTTP and Socket APIs[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo obtain a holistic understanding of this vulnerability, the following codebase [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be investigated:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor class** [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m316[0m[39m in stack trace[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m299[0m[39m in stack trace[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How XML parsing is configured and initialized for processing extended [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperties[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML Parser Configuration**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All locations where `SAXParser` instances are created or configured[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether external entity processing features are explicitly enabled or disabled[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Default configurations for XML parsing throughout the POI XSSF module[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Related XSSF Extractors**:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other extractor classes that may perform similar XML parsing operations[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Common XML parsing utilities or helper classes used across XSSF components[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Entity Resolution Handling**:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Custom entity resolvers, if any, implemented in the POI codebase[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - How external references in OOXML documents are intended to be handled[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Input Validation**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Whether there are any existing controls to validate or sanitize XML content [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore parsing[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security configurations or options available to users of the POI library[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Similar Vulnerability Patterns**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other file format parsers in POI [0m[1;39m([0m[39mHSSF, HWPF, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that might have similar [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML parsing patterns[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any previous security fixes related to XXE or SSRF in the POI project[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights from Code Snippets[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause Identified**: The `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod at line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m creates an insecure SAXParser using [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without any XXE/SSRF protection [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfigurations.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Security Infrastructure Exists**: The POI codebase has comprehensive security [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutilities:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`: Provides secure SAXParserFactory with all [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXXE protections[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`: Creates secure XMLReader with entity resolver[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These utilities disable external entities, DTD loading, and DOCTYPE [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclarations[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Inconsistency Within Same Class**: The `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` class [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses secure parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for sheet data in `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod but insecure parsing for extended properties in `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Redundant Parsing**: The vulnerable method re-parses XML that was already [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurely parsed by `POIXMLProperties` in the constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m96[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`properties` field already contains secure access to extended properties.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Test Flexibility**: Test cases use `[0m[1;35msnipProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to remove extended properties[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtext before assertions, indicating the exact format is not strictly tested and can [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe modified if needed.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Inherited Vulnerability**: `XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor` extends [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor`, inheriting the same vulnerability.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Extended Properties Extraction**: The method must continue to append extended [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperties to the text output when present[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: The general behavior of `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` must remain the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Exception Handling**: Silent exception swallowing pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m319[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be maintained to avoid breaking existing error handling[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Text Format**: While not strictly tested, maintaining a similar format [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[32m"Extended Properties:\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m minimizes potential impact[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix Approach: Replace Insecure SAXParser with Secure SAXParserFactory[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Method**: `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m308[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Steps to Implement**:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Replace the insecure SAXParser creation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m315[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with XMLHelper's secure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXParserFactory:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Change from:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Change to:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Add entity resolver for additional protection** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m, before line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   XMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mparser.getXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Note: This requires adjusting the parsing call since we're using XMLReader [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of SAXParser directly.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Update exception handling** to include the same exception types to maintain [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompatibility.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Specific Changes**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The method already imports `SAXParser` and `SAXParserFactory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m32[0m[1;39m)[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add import for `StringReader` if using entity resolver approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m22[0m[39m already[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhas relevant imports[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace lines [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[39m with secure parser initialization:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which provides a factory with:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING` enabled[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_LOAD_DTD_GRAMMAR` disabled[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD` disabled[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES` disabled[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL` enabled[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Modified Code Block** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m308[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    List<PackagePart> parts = [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcontainer.getPartsByRelationshipType[0m[1;39m([0m[39mEXTENDED_PROPERTIES[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparts == null || [0m[1;35mparts.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    PackagePart part = [0m[1;35mparts.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        XMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mparser.getXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException | SAXException | IOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95mswallow[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only modifies [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m lines in the vulnerable method, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreducing risk of introducing new bugs[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: Uses the same `XMLHelper` utility that the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclass already uses for secure sheet parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Functionality**: [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains the same text formatting through `ExtendedPropertiesHandler`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keeps the same exception handling behavior[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Doesn't break the existing test suite[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Security**: [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Applies all OWASP-recommended XXE protections[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adds entity resolver as defense-in-depth[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents both SSRF and local file access attacks[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Makes the extended properties parsing consistent with sheet [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing security standards in the same class[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No External Dependencies**: Uses existing POI security infrastructure without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequiring new dependencies[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible**: The output format and behavior remain unchanged, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining API compatibility[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **SSRF Prevention**: The secure SAXParserFactory disables external entity [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolution, preventing connections to external hosts like [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **XXE Prevention**: Disables DTD loading and DOCTYPE declarations, preventing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML External Entity attacks[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Entity Resolution**: The added entity resolver returns empty InputSource for [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many entity resolution attempts, providing defense-in-depth[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Stack Trace Path Fixed**: The vulnerable call chain through [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is blocked at the parser configuration level[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Malformed XML Handling**: If extended properties XML contains DOCTYPE [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclarations, parsing will now fail instead of processing them[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The existing catch block silently handles this [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m319[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaintaining current behavior[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Minimal - files with malicious DTDs would previously trigger SSRF,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow they're safely rejected[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: No measurable performance impact - the secure factory is cached[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min XMLHelper[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Entity References in Legitimate Files**: If legitimate Excel files contain [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references in extended properties [0m[1;39m([0m[39mextremely rare[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The entity resolver returns empty string, preventing errors [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile blocking external access[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Impact**: Entity values would be empty instead of resolved - acceptable [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity tradeoff[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Same Class Pattern**: The `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already uses [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` successfully[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Codebase Standards**: `XSSFImportFromXML` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m91[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mDocumentHelper.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for secure parsing[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Test Coverage**: `[0m[1;35mTestXMLHelper.testXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` verifies that secure parsers [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwork correctly with all security features enabled[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **OWASP Compliance**: The fix aligns with OWASP XXE Prevention Cheat Sheet [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferenced in XMLHelper [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: d9d032fd1efaa9d3[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue is a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability detected [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing of Apache POI's XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExcel file format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processing code. The [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability occurs when the XML parser attempts to resolve external entities, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to an attempted network connection to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m. The patch attempt [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtried to prevent this by configuring an entity resolver on the SAX parser to return[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty content for external entities. However, the patch failed to compile due to an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincorrect API usage - specifically calling `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with two arguments [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen it only accepts one.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability was triggered during the processing of XLSX files in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. The stack trace reveals [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe following flow:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The vulnerability originates at line [0m[1;36m316[0m[39m of `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.java` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere `[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The SAX parser processes XML content and encounters an entity reference[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. At `[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, the parser attempts [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto resolve the entity[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The entity resolution triggers network connectivity through [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. This results in an HTTP connection attempt to [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The SSRF detector intercepts the socket connection at [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mjava.net.Socket.connect[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and raises the security exception[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is classified as a medium-severity security issue because [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequests to untrusted destinations could lead to:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exfiltration of sensitive data[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Exposure of internal services[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Server-side request forgery attacks[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch modified [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/[0m[95mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtracto[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mr.java[0m[39m` in the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m312[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The changes [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincluded:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Added import**: `import java.io.StringReader;` to support the entity resolver [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Replaced SAXParser creation**: Changed from [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to use a centralized XML helper [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat presumably provides secure defaults[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Added entity resolver**: Configured a custom entity resolver that returns an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty `InputSource` for all external entities:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Modified parse invocation**: Attempted to change the parsing call to use [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLReader` directly instead of `SAXParser`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Compilation Failure[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch failed at the compilation stage with the following error:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/src/poi/poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/[0m[95mXSSFEventBasedExcelE[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mxtractor.java[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m319[0m[39m: error: no suitable method found for [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[39morg.xml.sax.InputSource,org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtr[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactor.ExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is that `[0m[1;35mXMLReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method only accepts a single `InputSource` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameter, but the patch attempted to pass two arguments: an `InputSource` and a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ContentHandler` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `ExtendedPropertiesHandler`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The correct approach would be [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto set the content handler separately using `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalling `[0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Further Investigation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
