[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Core Insights from Code Snippets[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause**: The `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m uses [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which creates a parser with default[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39minsecure[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m settings that allow external entity resolution, leading to the SSRF [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Failed Patch Issue**: The last patch attempted to use `[0m[1;35mXMLReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo arguments [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputSource and ContentHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but the XMLReader API only accepts [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma single InputSource parameter. The ContentHandler must be set separately using [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35msetContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Correct Pattern**: The codebase consistently uses this three-step pattern for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure XML parsing:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Create XMLReader via `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Set ContentHandler via `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mhandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parse with single argument via `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39minputStream[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Infrastructure**: [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` provides comprehensive security:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Uses `saxFactory` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpre-configured with secure defaults from [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mgetSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Sets entity resolver to return empty content: [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mxmlReader.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLHelper::ignoreEntity[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Disables external entities, DTD loading, and DOCTYPE declarations[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Sets entity expansion limits[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `[0m[1;35mignoreEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method returns `new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent external entity resolution[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Handler Compatibility**: `ExtendedPropertiesHandler` extends `DefaultHandler` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich implements `ContentHandler`, so it's fully compatible with the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` API.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Import Already Present**: The file already imports `XMLHelper` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m48[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLReader` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m65[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `ContentHandler` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and `InputSource` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m63[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno new imports are needed beyond what the failed patch already added.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability exists because:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m uses insecure `[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. No entity resolver is configured to prevent external entity resolution[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Security features [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES, FEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39metc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are not disabled[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Logic to Preserve[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The method must continue to parse extended properties from the [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEXTENDED_PROPERTIES package part[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The `ExtendedPropertiesHandler` must receive and process the SAX events to build[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe text output[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Exception handling must remain unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mswallowing [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mParserConfigurationException, SAXException, IOException[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. The try-with-resources pattern for the InputStream must be preserved[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File: [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`**[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Keep the StringReader import** from the failed patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready added[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   import java.io.StringReader;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Replace the vulnerable SAXParser approach** with the secure XMLReader pattern [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   **From:**[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   **To:**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       XMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Changes Explained[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: This provides a pre-configured secure [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXMLReader with:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entity resolver that returns empty content for all external entities[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disabled external entity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[33mFEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disabled DTD loading [0m[1;39m([0m[33mFEATURE_LOAD_DTD_GRAMMAR[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[39m, [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [33mFEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD[0m[39m=[0m[35mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disallowed DOCTYPE declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[33mFEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Entity expansion limits set to [0m[1;36m1[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Set ContentHandler separately**: Call `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to register the handler. This is the correct API [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39musage for XMLReader, unlike the failed patch which tried to pass the handler as a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecond argument to [0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Wrap InputStream in InputSource**: Call `[0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a single argument. This matches the XMLReader API signature and is consistent [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith how `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and other secure parsing methods in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase work.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Consistent with Codebase**: This exact pattern is used in `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, `XSSFReader` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m347[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m353[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and `ReadOnlySharedStringsTable` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m195[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m197[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Comprehensive Security**: Uses `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which provides [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefense-in-depth:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Factory-level security features from `[0m[1;35mgetSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reader-level entity resolver that blocks all external entities[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Additional security features and entity expansion limits[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Only modifies the vulnerable lines [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m314[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preserving:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The try-with-resources pattern[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Exception handling behavior[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ExtendedPropertiesHandler logic[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method signature and external interfaces[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The ExtendedPropertiesHandler receives the same SAX events[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method signature remains unchanged[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The text output format remains the same[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No impact on test compatibility[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes SSRF Vulnerability**: The entity resolver in `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturns empty content for all external entities, preventing the parser from making [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnetwork requests to resolve entities like [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes Compilation Error**: Uses the correct XMLReader API with three distinct [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msteps [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcreate reader, set handler, parse with InputSource[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of the incorrect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo-argument [0m[1;35mparse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m call from the failed patch.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Prevents XXE Attacks**: The comprehensive security features [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdisabled external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities, DTD processing, DOCTYPE declarations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m protect against all XML External [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEntity attack vectors.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m Expected**: This change only affects how the XML is parsed, not what is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed or how the SAX events are processed. The ExtendedPropertiesHandler receives [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentical events.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m has negligible overhead compared to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe insecure factory approach. The entity resolver check is very fast [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturns [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty InputSource immediately[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Compatibility**: This change is internal to the parsing logic. External [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallers of `[0m[1;35mgetText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and tests of `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` will see no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferences in behavior for legitimate XLSX files.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly mirrors the secure pattern used in:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.processSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m251[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m255[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `XSSFReader.SheetIterator` constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m347[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m353[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mReadOnlySharedStringsTable.readFrom[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m195[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m197[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mFromHowTo.fetchSheetParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexamples, lines [0m[1;36m81[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m83[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll these methods use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, set ContentHandler separately, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparse with a single InputSource argument.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
